ï¿½l     Volume 1\"""", ""\""
This volume contains information and tips for an aspiring Dungeoneer.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Gilded and Jewelled Equipment

By applying precious materials to your iron equipment, you can maintain it's effectiveness while gaining the benefits of the additional material(s).\"""", ""\""Gilded items will have increased enchantability and jewelled items will also have increased effectiveness. Aside from being more receptive of enchantments, gilded and jewelled armour sets are able to absorb a portion of magical damage.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l  Studded Armour

This is a cheaper upgrade from leather that provides the armour toughness effect. The dense material is good defence against explosions.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l  Battle Armour

This may seem like pointless armour, due to it's low surface area, but it is suprisingly effective at glancing even heavy blows off of the wearer.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Flight Goggles
ï¿½l and Rocket Pants

Who ever made these was probably just messing around and clearly has little concern for personal safety. When the gunpowder is ignited, the rockets will increase the wearers jump height to almost deadly heights.\"""", ""\""
It is possible to glide, by burning any remaining fumes, if the wearer has a pair of flight goggles equipped.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Bounce Boots

Self explanatory. You fall, they bounce. Hopefully with you still in them. If you fall like a rock, the impact will still hurt, but if you fall like a feather you may not feel the landing at all.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Magic Tether

A piece of rope, wrapped in space and tangled by the void. If one focusses while using this item it will violently pull them through space to a safe place. A lack of focus is likely to not take you far.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Phylactery

Containing the power of a fraction of a soul, this abhorrent machination of twisted minds is able to capture the soul of the one who holds it and force it back into their body, unnaturally healing them in the process.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l       Bag of
ï¿½l      Hoarding

Carrying an ender chest it just silly. Put it in a bag and you don't even have to put it down to open it.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Ducttape

It holds the universe and everything else together. Apply it to the item in your other hand and it will hold that together too, as long as there is something left to hold together.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Heart Drops

When defeated, creatures have a chance to drop concentrated life essence, which will be absorbed on contact and heal the one who touches it. Can be collected in a bottle.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Loot Bags

Stollen, lost, discarded, looted. Who knows where these bags of random stuff come from, but finders keepers.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l  Survival Rations

You'd be surprised what you are willing to eat when you are starving. Rotten flesh is not the best, but it can be made edible... Well, almost.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Potion Fish

Spilled potions of dead adventurers have to drain away somewhere. Sometimes that somewhere is waull of water, sometimes that water has fish. Over the years... Lets just say, a lot of people have died and these fish taste great.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Lanterns

This volume contains information on different weapons and their uses.

Section 1 contains melee weapons.
Section 2 contains imbuements.
Section 3 contains ranged weapons.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 1

ï¿½l   Melee Combat\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Mastery Tomes

Mastery Tomes allow the wielder to use special abilities with their melee weapon.
To activate this ability, you must use your held weapon with the tome in your inventory - most abilities cannot be used while holding a shield.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Swords

Swords and Cutlasses are the mid-ground weapon. Aveverage in both speed and offence.

The ability ï¿½lRiposteï¿½r allows the wielder to block and counter an incoming attack, when timed properly.\"""", ""\""
The ability ï¿½lPierceï¿½r allows the wielder to ignore a portion of the targets armour.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Hammers

Hammers hit hard, but have a slower attack speed than swords.

The ï¿½lLeapingï¿½r ability allows the wielder to propel themselves forward into, or out of, battle.\"""", ""\""
The ï¿½lSmashï¿½r ability creates an explosive force around the wielder, knocking back and damaging all foes.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Battleaxes

Battleaxes are like sharp hammers, still slow, but with a bit more damage.
Though this weapon type cannot be mastered, it has a good chance to decapitate foes.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Glaives

Glaives are the pointiest of pointy sticks, perfect for poking things at range.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Knives

Knives are built for speed, but lack the damage of larger blades.

The ï¿½lSmokeBombï¿½r ability allows the wielder to disappear briefly, to escape, or gain an advantage over a foe.\"""", ""\""
The ï¿½lMultistrikeï¿½r ability allows the wielder to dash to multiple targets and strike them all at once.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Cestus

A true berserker's weapon, this weapon can be swung as fast as you can punch.

The ï¿½lRoarï¿½r ability allows the wielder to unleash a primal rage, bolstering their strength, knocking back and stunning groups of attackers.\"""", ""\""
The ï¿½lPummelï¿½r ability allows the wielder to unleash a flurry of blows, dealing multiple strikes to a single target.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Shields

A portable wall, perfect for protecting your pretty little face from the ravages of combat. Also doubles as a tool to bash your foes away.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 2

ï¿½l      Imbuing\"""", ""\""
Other gateways to ultimate power are available.
Just light a fire below the cauldron, throw a flower in and stir with your weapon of choice.\"""", ""\""
Coating your wepon in poison is a quick and easy way to gain an advantage in combat, though it is temporary. Mix and match poisons for best results. Warrenty not included.\"""", ""\""
The combat orientated definitely want to keep an eye out for weapon enchantments, such as 'ï¿½lBerserkingï¿½r' which increases the weilder's damage the less armour the have, 'ï¿½lRunedï¿½r' which converts some physical damage dealt to magical damage.\"""", ""\""
'ï¿½lLife Stealï¿½r' which heals the wielder for a portion of the damage they deal, and ï¿½lSYNTAX ERRORï¿½r: Token not found (jk, I just didn't add it yet).\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    NotYetImplemented

ï¿½l     Section 3

ï¿½l  Ranged Combat\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Slingshot

The Slingshot is easy to make and easy to use. Allowing for a reasonable rate of fire but less damage than a bow.
Slingshots are capable of firing seeds, flint, and cherrybombs, each having a different effect on the target.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Potshot

Mechanically propelled ordinance at it's finest. The Potshot always fires at full power with decent impact damage.\"""", ""\""The versatile projectile morphs to the weapons enchantments, such as the 'ï¿½lExplodingï¿½r', 'ï¿½lBonus Packageï¿½r', or 'ï¿½lDebilitatingï¿½r' enchantments, causing anything from explosive damage, fragmenting projectiles, or caustic slime damage respectively.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Grenades

Light the fuse and throw or launch from a dispenser, grenades are excellent for crowd control. Letting the fuse burn for a bit, before throwing, will reduce the time the grenade takes to explode, but don't hold it too long.\"""", ""\""Adding certain ingredients to the mix imbues the granade with one of several effects.

ï¿½lBasic grenadesï¿½r explode, dealing damage to targets.

ï¿½lPyro grenadesï¿½r explode with fire, dealing slightly less immediate damage.\"""", ""\""
ï¿½lPorting grenadesï¿½r deal very low damage and teleport all targets away.

ï¿½lCryo grenadesï¿½r cause low damage and temporarily freeze targets. Frozen enemies take increased damage.\""""], author: ""Some probably-dead guy"", title: ""Weapons""})"

Despite there grim visage, the charms protect the user. They work in the similarly to Trinkets, except that they remove negative effects from the user and do not stay active.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l   Dungeonpedia

ï¿½l     Volume 3\"""", ""\""
This volume contains information on alchemy and magic scrolls. Grab your spoon.

Section 1 contains alchemy.
Section 2 contains magic scrolls.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 1

ï¿½l      Alchemy\"""", ""\""
Mixing items in a cauldron is your gateway to ultimate power!!! Or, like, some extra resources and stuff.
Just light a fire below the cauldron, throw the ingredients in and stir with your favourite spoon.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Cherrybombs

Actual cherries, that explode. They may only contain a small amount of a gunpowder like substance, but they are non-toxic and can be used to create quantities of real gunpowder.\"""", ""\""
Combine four of cherrybombs with four redstone dust, one flint, and water, in a cauldron, and stir with a spoon to create gunpowder.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l  Incindiberries

Kind of like a Persimmon, if the juice was lava. Really tasty and really good for your health, if you are immune to fire. Enough juice from these can melt magma. *recommond you do this in a bucket*\"""", ""\""
Combine seven of incindiberries with magma and a bucket, in a dry cauldron, and stir with a spoon to create lava. Add water to create obsidian.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Glowcurrent

If you don't mind everything knowing where you are, these peculiar berries can keep an unprepared traveller going through the Nether. Strangely harmless when eaten. I mean, I expected more death from Nether berries...\"""", ""\""
Combine four of glowcurrents with four redstone dust, one blaze powder, and water, in a cauldron, and stir with a spoon to create glowstone dust.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Magic Dust

A neccesary catalyst for casting spells, because you have no latent magical abilities. None. So you need to syphon power from actually magical sources.\"""", ""\""
Combine glowstone dust with a red mushroom, a brown mushroom, and water, in a cauldron, and stir with a spoon to create magic dust.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Golden Hearts

If you can capture a heart and smother it in gold, it won't love you back, but you can still eat it.\"""", ""\""
Combine a bottled heart with two gold nuggets and two glowstone dust, in a dry cauldron, and stir with a spoon to create a golden heart.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 2

ï¿½l   Magic Scrolls\"""", ""\""
Casting any spell will consume magic dust. Loose dust will be consumed even if the spell fails. so put it in a little baggy and your magic dust will be safe from your failures... Unless you die in lava, but that's a whole other story.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Magic Pouch

You could keep your magic dust up your sleeve, or in your belly button, but these nifty little pouches can hold a lot more. Just open it up and it will automatically eat magic dust from your pockets.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Concentration

Most spells have two casting modes. Concentrating (sneaking) will change the effect, causeing some spells to cast as an AoE, or ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Mage Affinity

The Mage Affinity enchantment takes the embued magical properties of the enchanted armour and reduces the cost of casting spells.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Restoration

Normal cast will heal the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will heal the caster and ALL in range, for about half the amount.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Satiate

Normal cast will feed the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will feed the caster and ALL in range, for about half the amount.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Forging

Normal cast will smelt all ores and some other resources in the caster's pockets, concentration cast will smelt one stack but produce double the output.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Cooking

Normal cast will cook all food in the caster's pockets, concentration cast will cook one stack but produce double the output.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Freezing

Normal cast will apply slowness and cryo to all targets, except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Uncover

Normal cast will remove armour from all targets except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l       Disarm

Normal cast will cause all targets, except the caster and team-mates, to drop held items, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Disorient

Normal cast will spin and blind all targets, except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l       Punish

Normal cast will deal magic damage all targets, except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l       Wither

Normal cast will apply wither all targets, except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l        Smite

Normal cast will invoke lightning on all targets, except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Magic Missile

Normal cast will launch a homing projectile all targets, except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Pin Missile

Basically what happens if a porkupine sneezes really hard.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Transport

Ever wanted a dead horse? Well that's what you get, so quit yer yappin'.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Companion

Did your best friend die? Life's not fair, but magic plays dirty.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l       Sunder

Normal cast deals heavy damage to all targets, except the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will ignore other players.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l        Rage

Normal cast apply strength and resistance to the caster and team-mates, concentration cast will buff the caster and ALL in range, for about half the amount.\""""], author: ""Some probably-dead guy"", title: ""Magic and Alchemy""})"

ï¿½l     Volume 5\"""", ""\""
This volume contains information on the unique equipment that have survived the ages. Each of these items carry a powerful benefit, but nothing is perfect.\"""", ""\""
The powerful magic present in these ancient items prevents them from further enchantment, and requires special materials to repair.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   High Striker

Once a simple mallet used in a carnival game, this weapon has gained the curious ability to throw hit entities into the air and ring the bell.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Wackerjab

Each jab, or whack, with this weapon will impart pure entropy on a living target.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Taser

Able to summon lightning on to any hit foe, this weapon poses as much threat to the weilder as it does the victim.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Claws

Perfect for a berserker, these knuckle knives will keep the weilder healed, but you have to keep yourself fed.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Lithen Scythe

This ominous weapon was specifically made, by an impartial force, to collect the souls of the living. When an entity is killed with this farming tool, a part of their life-force will temporarily bolster the user's spirit.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Hï¿½hnerfeder

The immense power of the being that this feather came from is able to bring forth mighty minions to aid the weilder in combat.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Pirate Hook

The prosthetic excuse for a hand of an old pirate with a lust for gold. Legends say that his riches would last as long as he could fight.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Coin Cannon

Ever been so cold that you would burn money just to stay warm? This is that, but weaponised.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l Backfire Cannon

A well used, old, Potshot. The condition is still good, but the barrel is clogged with decades of gunpowder. A short in the redstone firing mechanism causes a powerful blast, spraying smoke and embers all around the user.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Fire Water

Very aged. Probably not safe to drink. Might not set you on fire. Sounds like fun.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Boots of
ï¿½l  Blinding Speed

Able to envigorate the wearer, allowing them to move at phenominal speeds.
Some say that these boots came from a volcano island in a distant province.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Icarus Ring

Everybody wants to fly... Or was it die?\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    NotYetImplemented
    MysteryShenanigans\""""], author: ""Some probably-dead guy"", title: ""Unique Weapons""})"

ï¿½l   Dungeonpedia

ï¿½l     Volume 6\"""", ""\""
This volume contains information on tools and traps to help you build your own defences and hinder those that may invade your own dungeon.

Section 1 contains tools.
Section 2 contains traps.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 1

ï¿½l       Tools\"""", ""\""ï¿½lEngineer's Clothes

An essential outfit for any dungeon engineer. These specially designed clothes, while not good protection in combat, will protect you from the effects of traps.\"""", ""\""ï¿½lEngineer's Wrench

A dungeon engineer's primary tool; the wrench can be used to rotate blocks, such as pistons and fans, and is excellent for picking up such blocks and rails\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Portable
ï¿½l   Piston Device
Pistons are great, but not always convenient.
Putting the pushing power of a piston in your hand, this device will let you quickly reposition those misplaced blocks before anyone notices.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Portable
ï¿½l Tunnelling Device
Also known as the Boom Glove, this device is the result of too many broken picks and a surplus of gunpowder. Using this device will allow the wielder to blast their way through walls and rocks, while preserving most ores encountered.\"""", ""\""
The 'ï¿½lBigger Boomï¿½r' enchantment will increse the power of the PTD's tunneling capabilities, while the 'ï¿½lSonic Boomï¿½r' enchantment will modify the tool to use magically generated sound waves, instead of gunpowder, to create explosions.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 2

ï¿½l      Devices
ï¿½l     and Traps\"""", ""\""ï¿½l  Powered Fence

The redstone dust applied to this metal fencing creates a buildup of charge which will be discharged into any creature that touches it.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l        Fans

Strong enough to push items, creatures, and other people, these fans make a great alternative to water in mob traps, as well as elevators.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l       Flamer

Unable to push entities, this little beauty set things on fire instead.
Manufacturer's notice; may start fires. Use at user's own risk.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Trap Plates

A self contained trap that activates when stepped on. Some traps will cause damage, while others aim to disorient invaders.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Dispensers

No tweaking necessary, dispensers can be used for a variety of utilities, such as using weapons, shearing sheep, and milking cows.\""""], author: ""Some probably-dead guy"", title: ""Engineering""})"
"<dungeontactics:dungeonpedia:8>.withTag({pages: [""\""

ï¿½l   Dungeonpedia

ï¿½l     Volume 7\"""", ""\""
This volume contains information on structures and other dangers of the world.

Section 1 contains structures.
Section 2 contains flowers.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 1

ï¿½l    Structures\"""", ""\""ï¿½l    Structures

Abandoned and swarming with creatures that want to kill you. These are good places to find forgotten loot, but they are likely trapped.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Towers

Built high into the sky, these monuments are so run down that the windows are stained to the point where they block light from entering.\"""", ""\""
Placing a skull on the alter found atop these towers will summon an ancient guardian who can be challenged to a fight to the death for a chance at his prize.\"""", ""\""ï¿½l     Dungeons

Submerged under the soil and rock, some of the dungeons can run long and deep beneath the surface. Before being abandoned, the original inhabitants left a golem to prevent monsters from overrunning the land.\"""", ""\""
*Dev note: dungeons are not finished, but are fully functional*\"""", ""\""ï¿½l   Pirate Ships

The undead crews of these drifting vessels are doomed to protect the ships ill gotten goods until the end of their unnatural life. The captain may be long dead, but his plunder may still be hidden on board.\"""", ""\""

ï¿½l     Section 2

ï¿½l      Flowers\"""", ""\""ï¿½l      Flowers

Throughout the land, nature fights back against the spread of man and monster kind alike. Some flowers have evolved their own defences, some aiding creatures, in hope of protection, others harming any how come to close.\"""", ""\""
These flowers seem to spread like fungus and can be farmed for resource cheap utilities.\""""], author: ""Some probably-dead guy"", title: ""World""})"
